;;; ARGS*: -v --enable-threads --enable-saturating-float-to-int --enable-sign-extension --enable-simd --enable-tail-call
;;; ARGS1: --host-print

(module
  (import "host" "print" (func $print (param i32)))

  (type $empty (func))
  (func $empty)
  (memory 1 1 shared)
  (table anyfunc (elem $empty $empty))
